 // If all zeros, use a large value\n  } else {\n    // Count leading zeros + 1\n    while ((remaining & (1ULL << (63 - (rho - 1)))) == 0 && rho <= 64) {\n      rho++;\n    }\n  }\n\n  {\n    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n    UpdateBuckets(bucket_idx, rho);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Use the harmonic mean formula from HyperLogLog paper\n  double raw_estimate = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    uint64_t val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    // Check if there's an overflow value\n    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {\n      val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    }\n    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(val));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula\n  double alpha = CONSTANT;\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(alpha * m * m / raw_estimate);\n}"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":464,"cache_read_input_tokens":48325,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":464},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c8896a93-3db2-4a88-9f55-8929d67011df","uuid":"88101be0-f589-4076-bcee-34ba934ad827"}

That's still not matching the expected value of 2.\n\nWait, what if I'm supposed to count trailing zeros instead of leading zeros? Using __builtin_ctzll on 131072 gives 17, so rho would be 18. When I mask that to 4 bits (18 & 0xF), I get 2—exactly what I need. This suggests the Presto implementation might be using trailing zero counting rather than the leading zero
